# Design Specification for OnlineCourse Web Application

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)

| Route Path                      | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template File            | Context Variables                                   |
|--------------------------------|-------------------------|-------------|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| /                              | root                    | GET         | N/A (redirect to dashboard) | None                                                |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard               | GET         | dashboard.html           | username: str, fullname: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int}) |
| /catalog                      | catalog                 | GET         | catalog.html             | username: str, courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str})                      |
| /course/<int:course_id>        | course_details          | GET, POST   | course_details.html      | username: str, course: dict ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str, category: str, level: str, duration: str, status: str}), already_enrolled: bool |
| /my-courses                   | my_courses              | GET         | my_courses.html          | username: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int, status: str})   |
| /learn/<int:course_id>          | course_learning         | GET, POST   | course_learning.html     | username: str, course: dict, lessons: list of dicts ({lesson_id: int, title: str, content: str}), current_lesson: dict, progress: int, can_mark_complete: bool |
| /assignments                  | my_assignments          | GET         | assignments.html         | username: str, assignments: list of dicts ({assignment_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, description: str, due_date: str, max_points: int}), submissions: dict {assignment_id: submission dict or None} |
| /submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id> | submit_assignment       | GET, POST   | submit_assignment.html   | username: str, assignment: dict ({assignment_id: int, title: str, description: str}), submission_status: str or None |
| /certificates                 | certificates            | GET         | certificates.html        | username: str, certificates: list of dicts ({certificate_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, issue_date: str}) |
| /profile                     | profile                 | GET, POST   | profile.html             | username: str, email: str, fullname: str |

### Route Behavior Notes:
- The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress.
- POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry.
- POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt.
- POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)

### 1. dashboard.html
- File Path: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Learning Dashboard (in <title> and <h1>)
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page (div container)
  - welcome-message (h1 displaying: "Welcome, {{ fullname }}")
  - enrolled-courses (div for listing enrolled courses)
  - browse-courses-button (button with url_for('catalog'))
  - my-courses-button (button with url_for('my_courses'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - fullname (str)
  - enrolled_courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, progress: int})
- Navigation:
  - browse-courses-button -> url_for('catalog')
  - my-courses-button -> url_for('my_courses')

### 2. catalog.html
- File Path: templates/catalog.html
- Page Title: Available Courses
- Element IDs:
  - catalog-page (div container)
  - search-input (input for search)
  - course-grid (div contains course cards)
  - view-course-button-{course_id} (button repeated for each course with id using Jinja: "view-course-button-{{ course.course_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, description: str})
- Navigation:
  - view-course-button-{course_id} -> url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

### 3. course_details.html
- File Path: templates/course_details.html
- Page Title: Course Details
- Element IDs:
  - course-details-page (div container)
  - course-title (h1 showing course.title)
  - course-description (div showing course.description)
  - enroll-button (button)
  - back-to-catalog (button with url_for('catalog'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - course (dict with course data fields)
  - already_enrolled (bool)
- Navigation & Button State:
  - enroll-button -> POST to url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)
  - enroll-button text: "Enroll" if not enrolled, "Already Enrolled" if enrolled
  - enroll-button disabled if already_enrolled == True
  - back-to-catalog -> url_for('catalog')

### 4. my_courses.html
- File Path: templates/my_courses.html
- Page Title: My Courses
- Element IDs:
  - my-courses-page (div container)
  - courses-list (div listing enrolled courses)
  - continue-learning-button-{course_id} (button repeated; id="continue-learning-button-{{ course.course_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - enrolled_courses (list of dicts with course_id, title, progress, status)
- Navigation:
  - continue-learning-button-{course_id} -> url_for('course_learning', course_id=course.course_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

### 5. course_learning.html
- File Path: templates/course_learning.html
- Page Title: Course Learning
- Element IDs:
  - learning-page (div container)
  - lessons-list (div listing lessons)
  - lesson-content (div showing current lesson content)
  - mark-complete-button (button)
  - back-to-my-courses (button with url_for('my_courses'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - course (dict)
  - lessons (list of dicts with lesson_id:int, title:str, content:str)
  - current_lesson (dict with lesson_id, title, content)
  - progress (int)
  - can_mark_complete (bool)
- Navigation & Button State:
  - mark-complete-button -> POST to url_for('course_learning', course_id=course.course_id)
  - mark-complete-button disabled if can_mark_complete == False
  - back-to-my-courses -> url_for('my_courses')

### 6. assignments.html
- File Path: templates/assignments.html
- Page Title: My Assignments
- Element IDs:
  - assignments-page (div container)
  - assignments-table (table containing assignments)
  - submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id} (button repeated; id="submit-assignment-button-{{ assignment.assignment_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - assignments (list of dicts: assignment_id, course_id, title, description, due_date, max_points)
  - submissions (dict with assignment_id keys, values: submission dict or None)
- Navigation:
  - submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id} -> url_for('submit_assignment', assignment_id=assignment.assignment_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')
- Button State:
  - submit-assignment-button is enabled only if assignment submission is not done yet or is late

### 7. submit_assignment.html
- File Path: templates/submit_assignment.html
- Page Title: Submit Assignment
- Element IDs:
  - submit-page (div container)
  - assignment-info (div showing assignment title and description)
  - submission-text (textarea input)
  - submit-button (button to submit form)
  - back-to-assignments (button with url_for('my_assignments'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - assignment (dict: assignment_id, title, description)
  - submission_status (str or None for confirmation)
- Form:
  - POST form to url_for('submit_assignment', assignment_id=assignment.assignment_id)

### 8. certificates.html
- File Path: templates/certificates.html
- Page Title: My Certificates
- Element IDs:
  - certificates-page (div container)
  - certificates-grid (div grid of certificates)
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - certificates (list of dicts: certificate_id, course_id, title, issue_date)
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

### 9. profile.html
- File Path: templates/profile.html
- Page Title: My Profile
- Element IDs:
  - profile-page (div container)
  - profile-email (input for email)
  - profile-fullname (input for full name)
  - update-profile-button (button to save changes)
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - email (str)
  - fullname (str)
- Form:
  - POST form to url_for('profile')

## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)

### 1. users.txt
- File Path: data/users.txt
- Format: username|email|fullname
- Fields:
  - username: user's unique login name
  - email: user email address
  - fullname: full name of user
- Example Lines:
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner

### 2. courses.txt
- File Path: data/courses.txt
- Format: course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status
- Fields:
  - course_id: unique course identifier (int)
  - title: course title
  - description: full course description
  - category: course category (e.g., Programming, Web, Data)
  - level: difficulty level (e.g., Beginner, Intermediate, Advanced)
  - duration: estimated course duration (e.g., "40 hours")
  - status: current course status (e.g., Active)
- Example Lines:
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active

### 3. enrollments.txt
- File Path: data/enrollments.txt
- Format: enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status
- Fields:
  - enrollment_id: unique enrollment identifier (int)
  - username: user login
  - course_id: course identifier
  - enrollment_date: ISO format date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - progress: integer percentage (0-100)
  - status: enrollment status (e.g., In Progress, Completed)
- Example Lines:
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress

### 4. assignments.txt
- File Path: data/assignments.txt
- Format: assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points
- Fields:
  - assignment_id: unique assignment identifier (int)
  - course_id: related course identifier
  - title: assignment title
  - description: detailed description
  - due_date: ISO date for submission deadline
  - max_points: maximum points achievable (int)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200

### 5. submissions.txt
- File Path: data/submissions.txt
- Format: submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback
- Fields:
  - submission_id: unique submission identifier (int)
  - assignment_id: assignment identifier
  - username: submitting user
  - submission_text: text response submitted
  - submit_date: ISO date of submission
  - grade: numeric grade (int or empty)
  - feedback: text feedback (empty if none)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!

### 6. certificates.txt
- File Path: data/certificates.txt
- Format: certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date
- Fields:
  - certificate_id: unique certificate identifier (int)
  - username: user who earned certificate
  - course_id: course identifier
  - issue_date: ISO date certificate was issued
- Example Lines:
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['DATA_DIR'] = 'data'

# Helper functions for file handling

def read_file(filename):
    path = os.path.join(app.config['DATA_DIR'], filename)
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return []
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        lines = f.read().strip().split('\n')
        return [line.split('|') for line in lines if line.strip()]


def write_file(filename, lines):
    path = os.path.join(app.config['DATA_DIR'], filename)
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for line in lines:
            f.write('|'.join(str(x) for x in line) + '\n')


def get_user(username):
    users = read_file('users.txt')
    for user in users:
        if user[0] == username:
            return {'username': user[0], 'email': user[1], 'fullname': user[2]}
    return None


def get_courses():
    courses = read_file('courses.txt')
    course_list = []
    for c in courses:
        course_list.append({
            'course_id': int(c[0]),
            'title': c[1],
            'description': c[2],
            'category': c[3],
            'level': c[4],
            'duration': c[5],
            'status': c[6] if len(c) > 6 else ''
        })
    return course_list


def get_enrollments(username):
    enrollments = read_file('enrollments.txt')
    user_enroll = []
    for e in enrollments:
        if e[1] == username:
            user_enroll.append({
                'enrollment_id': int(e[0]),
                'username': e[1],
                'course_id': int(e[2]),
                'enroll_date': e[3],
                'progress': int(e[4]),
                'status': e[5]
            })
    return user_enroll


def save_enrollment(enrollment):
    enrollments = read_file('enrollments.txt')
    enrollment_found = False
    for i, e in enumerate(enrollments):
        if e[0] == str(enrollment['enrollment_id']):
            enrollments[i] = [str(enrollment['enrollment_id']), enrollment['username'], str(enrollment['course_id']), enrollment['enroll_date'], str(enrollment['progress']), enrollment['status']]
            enrollment_found = True
            break
    if not enrollment_found:
        enrollments.append([str(enrollment['enrollment_id']), enrollment['username'], str(enrollment['course_id']), enrollment['enroll_date'], str(enrollment['progress']), enrollment['status']])
    write_file('enrollments.txt', enrollments)


def get_next_enrollment_id():
    enrollments = read_file('enrollments.txt')
    if enrollments:
        max_id = max(int(enr[0]) for enr in enrollments)
        return max_id + 1
    else:
        return 1


def get_assignments():
    assignments = read_file('assignments.txt')
    assignment_list = []
    for a in assignments:
        assignment_list.append({
            'assignment_id': int(a[0]),
            'course_id': int(a[1]),
            'title': a[2],
            'description': a[3],
            'due_date': a[4],
            'max_points': int(a[5])
        })
    return assignment_list


def get_submissions():
    submissions = read_file('submissions.txt')
    submission_list = []
    for s in submissions:
        submission_list.append({
            'submission_id': s[0],
            'assignment_id': int(s[1]),
            'username': s[2],
            'submission_text': s[3],
            'submission_date': s[4],
            'score': int(s[5]),
            'feedback': s[6] if len(s) > 6 else ''
        })
    return submission_list


def save_submission(submission):
    submissions = read_file('submissions.txt')
    # Remove old submission if exists for same assignment and user
    submissions = [s for s in submissions if not (s[1] == str(submission['assignment_id']) and s[2] == submission['username'])]
    submissions.append([
        str(submission.get('submission_id', '')),
        str(submission['assignment_id']),
        submission['username'],
        submission['submission_text'],
        submission['submission_date'],
        str(submission['score']),
        submission.get('feedback', '')
    ])
    write_file('submissions.txt', submissions)


def get_next_certificate_id():
    certificates = read_file('certificates.txt')
    if certificates:
        max_id = max(int(c[0]) for c in certificates)
        return max_id + 1
    else:
        return 1


def get_certificates(username):
    certificates = read_file('certificates.txt')
    user_certs = []
    for c in certificates:
        if c[1] == username:
            user_certs.append({
                'certificate_id': int(c[0]),
                'username': c[1],
                'course_id': int(c[2]),
                'title': c[3],
                'issue_date': c[4]
            })
    return user_certs


def save_certificate(certificate):
    certificates = read_file('certificates.txt')
    certificates.append([
        str(certificate['certificate_id']),
        certificate['username'],
        str(certificate['course_id']),
        certificate['title'],
        certificate['issue_date']
    ])
    write_file('certificates.txt', certificates)


# Routes

@app.route('/')
def root():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard', username='john'))  # Default for demo


@app.route('/dashboard/<username>')
def dashboard(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    enrolled_courses = []
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    courses = get_courses()
    for enrollment in enrollments:
        course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == enrollment['course_id']), None)
        if course:
            enrolled_courses.append({
                'course_id': course['course_id'],
                'title': course['title'],
                'progress': enrollment['progress']
            })
    return render_template('dashboard.html', fullname=user['fullname'], enrolled_courses=enrolled_courses)


@app.route('/catalog')
def catalog():
    courses = get_courses()
    return render_template('catalog.html', courses=courses)


@app.route('/course/<int:course_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def course_details(course_id):
    courses = get_courses()
    course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == course_id), None)
    if not course:
        abort(404)
    # use a default username for demo, better with session management
    username = request.args.get('username', 'john')
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    currently_enrolled = any(e['course_id'] == course_id for e in enrollments)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        if not currently_enrolled:
            # Enroll user
            new_enrollment_id = get_next_enrollment_id()
            new_enrollment = {
                'enrollment_id': new_enrollment_id,
                'username': username,
                'course_id': course_id,
                'enroll_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                'progress': 0,
                'status': 'In Progress'
            }
            save_enrollment(new_enrollment)
            return redirect(url_for('my_courses', username=username))
    # If GET
    return render_template('course_details.html', course=course, username=username, already_enrolled=currently_enrolled)


@app.route('/my-courses/<username>')
def my_courses(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    courses = get_courses()
    enrolled_courses = []
    for enrollment in enrollments:
        course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == enrollment['course_id']), None)
        if course:
            enrolled_courses.append({
                'course_id': course['course_id'],
                'title': course['title'],
                'progress': enrollment['progress'],
                'status': enrollment['status']
            })
    return render_template('my_courses.html', username=username, enrolled_courses=enrolled_courses)


@app.route('/learn/<int:course_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def course_learning(course_id):
    username = request.args.get('username', 'john')
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    courses = get_courses()
    course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == course_id), None)
    if not course:
        abort(404)
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    enrollment = next((e for e in enrollments if e['course_id'] == course_id), None)
    if enrollment is None:
        abort(403)  # Not enrolled

    # For simplicity, dummy lessons list (should come from files or DB in real app)
    lessons = [
        {'lesson_id': 1, 'title': 'Lesson 1', 'content': 'Content of lesson 1'},
        {'lesson_id': 2, 'title': 'Lesson 2', 'content': 'Content of lesson 2'},
        {'lesson_id': 3, 'title': 'Lesson 3', 'content': 'Content of lesson 3'}
    ]
    progress = enrollment['progress']
    current_index = min(progress // 33, len(lessons) - 1) if progress > 0 else 0
    current_lesson = lessons[current_index]
    complete = False

    if request.method == 'POST':
        new_progress = min(progress + 33, 100)
        enrollment['progress'] = new_progress
        if new_progress == 100:
            enrollment['status'] = 'Completed'
            # Issue certificate
            certs = get_certificates(username)
            already_certified = any(c['course_id'] == course_id for c in certs)
            if not already_certified:
                new_cert_id = get_next_certificate_id()
                certificate = {
                    'certificate_id': new_cert_id,
                    'username': username,
                    'course_id': course_id,
                    'title': course['title'],
                    'issue_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                }
                save_certificate(certificate)
        save_enrollment(enrollment)
        progress = enrollment['progress']
        current_index = min(progress // 33, len(lessons) - 1) if progress > 0 else 0
        current_lesson = lessons[current_index]
        complete = (progress == 100)

    return render_template('course_learning.html', username=username, course=course, lessons=lessons, current_lesson=current_lesson, progress=progress, complete=complete)


@app.route('/assignments/<username>')
def my_assignments(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    assignments = get_assignments()
    submissions = get_submissions()
    submissions_dict = {}
    for a in assignments:
        submission = next((s for s in submissions if s['assignment_id'] == a['assignment_id'] and s['username'] == username), None)
        submissions_dict[a['assignment_id']] = submission
    return render_template('assignments.html', username=username, assignments=assignments, submissions=submissions_dict)


@app.route('/submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def submit_assignment(assignment_id):
    username = request.args.get('username', 'john')
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    assignments = get_assignments()
    assignment = next((a for a in assignments if a['assignment_id'] == assignment_id), None)
    if not assignment:
        abort(404)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        submission_text = request.form.get('submission_text', '')
        submission_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
        # Score and feedback default 0 and empty
        submission = {
            'assignment_id': assignment_id,
            'username': username,
            'submission_text': submission_text,
            'submission_date': submission_date,
            'score': 0,
            'feedback': ''
        }
        save_submission(submission)
        return redirect(url_for('my_assignments', username=username))
    return render_template('submit_assignment.html', assignment=assignment, username=username)


@app.route('/certificates/<username>')
def certificates(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    certificates_list = get_certificates(username)
    return render_template('certificates.html', username=username, certificates=certificates_list)


@app.route('/profile/<username>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def profile(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        fullname = request.form.get('fullname', '')
        email = request.form.get('email', '')
        # Update user data
        users = read_file('users.txt')
        for i, u in enumerate(users):
            if u[0] == username:
                users[i] = [username, email, fullname]
                break
        write_file('users.txt', users)
        return redirect(url_for('profile', username=username))
    return render_template('profile.html', fullname=user['fullname'], email=user['email'])


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(port=5000, debug=True)

Route Behavior Notes: - The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`. - POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress. - POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry. - POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt. - POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.  ---  ## Section username: user's unique login name   - email: user email address   - fullname: full name of user - Example Lines:   john|john@student.com|John Student   alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor   jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner  ### 2. courses.txt - File Path: data/courses.txt - Format: course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status - Fields:   - course_id: unique course identifier (int)   - title: course title   - description: full course description   - category: course category (e.g., Programming, Web, Data)   - level: difficulty level (e.g., Beginner, Intermediate, Advanced)   - duration: estimated course duration (e.g., "40 hours")   - status: current course status (e.g., Active) - Example Lines:   1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active   2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active   3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active  ### 3. enrollments.txt - File Path: data/enrollments.txt - Format: enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status - Fields:   - enrollment_id: unique enrollment identifier (int)   - username: user login   - course_id: course identifier   - enrollment_date: ISO format date (YYYY-MM-DD)   - progress: integer percentage (0-100)   - status: enrollment status (e.g., In Progress, Completed) - Example Lines:   1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress   2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed   3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress  ### 4. assignments.txt - File Path: data/assignments.txt - Format: assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points - Fields:   - assignment_id: unique assignment identifier (int)   - course_id: related course identifier   - title: assignment title   - description: detailed description   - due_date: ISO date for submission deadline   - max_points: maximum points achievable (int) - Example Lines:   1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100   2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200  ### 5. submissions.txt - File Path: data/submissions.txt - Format: submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback - Fields:   - submission_id: unique submission identifier (int)   - assignment_id: assignment identifier   - username: submitting user   - submission_text: text response submitted   - submit_date: ISO date of submission   - grade: numeric grade (int or empty)   - feedback: text feedback (empty if none) - Example Lines:   1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!   2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!  ### 6. certificates.txt - File Path: data/certificates.txt - Format: certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date - Fields:   - certificate_id: unique certificate identifier (int)   - username: user who earned certificate   - course_id: course identifier   - issue_date: ISO date certificate was issued - Example Lines:   1|jane|1|2024-11-22
  [app.py] from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort from datetime import datetime import os  app = Flask(__name__) app.config['DATA_DIR'] = 'data'  # Helper functions for reading and writing files  def read_file(filename):     path = os.path.join(app.config['DATA_DIR'], filename)     if not os.path.exists(path):         return []     with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:         return [line.strip().split('|') for line in f if line.strip()]   def write_file(filename, lines):     path = os.path.join(app.config['DATA_DIR'], filename)     with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:         for line in lines:             f.write('|'.join(str(x) for x in line) + '\n')   def get_user(username):     users = read_file('users.txt')     for u in users:         if u[0] == username:             return {'username': u[0], 'email': u[1], 'fullname': u[2]}     return None   def get_courses():     courses = read_file('courses.txt')     res = []     for c in courses:         res.append({             'course_id': int(c[0]),             'title': c[1],             'description': c[2],             'category': c[3],             'level': c[4],             'duration': c[5],             'status': c[6] if len(c) > 6 else ''         })     return res   def get_enrollments(username):     enrolls = read_file('enrollments.txt')     user_enrolls = []     for e in enrolls:         if e[1] == username:             user_enrolls.append({                 'enrollment_id': int(e[0]),                 'username': e[1],                 'course_id': int(e[2]),                 'enroll_date': e[3],                 'progress': int(e[4]),                 'status': e[5]             })     return user_enrolls   def get_enrollment(username, course_id):     enrollments = get_enrollments(username)     for e in enrollments:         if e['course_id'] == course_id:             return e     return None   def save_enrollments(enrollments):     lines = []     for e in enrollments:         lines.append([             str(e['enrollment_id']), e['username'], str(e['course_id']), e['enroll_date'], str(e['progress']), e['status']         ])     write_file('enrollments.txt', lines)   def get_assignments():     assigns = read_file('assignments.txt')     res = []     for a in assigns:         res.append({             'assignment_id': int(a[0]),             'course_id': int(a[1]),             'title': a[2],             'description': a[3],             'due_date': a[4],             'max_points': int(a[5])         })     return res   def get_submissions():     subs = read_file('submissions.txt')     res = []     for s in subs:         res.append({             'submission_id': s[0],             'assignment_id': int(s[1]),             'username': s[2],             'submission_text': s[3],             'submit_date': s[4],             'grade': int(s[5]),             'feedback': s[6] if len(s) > 6 else ''         })     return res   def save_submissions(submissions):     lines = []     for s in submissions:         lines.append([             s['submission_id'], str(s['assignment_id']), s['username'], s['submission_text'], s['submit_date'], str(s['grade']), s.get('feedback', '')         ])     write_file('submissions.txt', lines)   def get_certificates(username):     certs = read_file('certificates.txt')     res = []     for c in certs:         if c[1] == username:             res.append({                 'certificate_id': int(c[0]),                 'username': c[1],                 'course_id': int(c[2]),                 'issue_date': c[3]             })     return res   def save_certificate(certificate):     certs = read_file('certificates.txt')     certs.append([         str(certificate['certificate_id']),         certificate['username'],         str(certificate['course_id']),         certificate['issue_date']     ])     write_file('certificates.txt', certs)   def get_next_enrollment_id():     enrolls = # Design Specification for OnlineCourse Web Application

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)

| Route Path                      | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template File            | Context Variables                                   |
|--------------------------------|-------------------------|-------------|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| /                              | root                    | GET         | N/A (redirect to dashboard) | None                                                |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard               | GET         | dashboard.html           | username: str, fullname: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int}) |
| /catalog                      | catalog                 | GET         | catalog.html             | username: str, courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str})                      |
| /course/<int:course_id>        | course_details          | GET, POST   | course_details.html      | username: str, course: dict ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str, category: str, level: str, duration: str, status: str}), already_enrolled: bool |
| /my-courses                   | my_courses              | GET         | my_courses.html          | username: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int, status: str})   |
| /learn/<int:course_id>          | course_learning         | GET, POST   | course_learning.html     | username: str, course: dict, lessons: list of dicts ({lesson_id: int, title: str, content: str}), current_lesson: dict, progress: int, can_mark_complete: bool |
| /assignments                  | my_assignments          | GET         | assignments.html         | username: str, assignments: list of dicts ({assignment_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, description: str, due_date: str, max_points: int}), submissions: dict {assignment_id: submission dict or None} |
| /submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id> | submit_assignment       | GET, POST   | submit_assignment.html   | username: str, assignment: dict ({assignment_id: int, title: str, description: str}), submission_status: str or None |
| /certificates                 | certificates            | GET         | certificates.html        | username: str, certificates: list of dicts ({certificate_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, issue_date: str}) |
| /profile                     | profile                 | GET, POST   | profile.html             | username: str, email: str, fullname: str |

### Route Behavior Notes:
- The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress.
- POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry.
- POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt.
- POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)

### 1. dashboard.html
- File Path: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Learning Dashboard (in <title> and <h1>)
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page (div container)
  - welcome-message (h1 displaying: "Welcome, {{ fullname }}")
  - enrolled-courses (div for listing enrolled courses)
  - browse-courses-button (button with url_for('catalog'))
  - my-courses-button (button with url_for('my_courses'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - fullname (str)
  - enrolled_courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, progress: int})
- Navigation:
  - browse-courses-button -> url_for('catalog')
  - my-courses-button -> url_for('my_courses')

  - course-grid (div contains course cards)
  - view-course-button-{course_id} (button repeated for each course with id using Jinja: "view-course-button-{{ course.course_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))

  - username (str)
  - courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, description: str})

  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

  - enroll-button (button)

  - enroll-button -> POST to url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)

## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)

### 1. users.txt
- File Path: data/users.txt
- Format: username|email|fullname
- Fields:
  - username: user's unique login name
  - email: user email address
  - fullname: full name of user
- Example Lines:
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner

### 2. courses.txt
- File Path: data/courses.txt
- Format: course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status
- Fields:
  - course_id: unique course identifier (int)
  - title: course title
  - description: full course description
  - category: course category (e.g., Programming, Web, Data)
  - level: difficulty level (e.g., Beginner, Intermediate, Advanced)
  - duration: estimated course duration (e.g., "40 hours")
  - status: current course status (e.g., Active)
- Example Lines:
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active

### 3. enrollments.txt
- File Path: data/enrollments.txt
- Format: enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status
- Fields:
  - enrollment_id: unique enrollment identifier (int)
  - username: user login
  - course_id: course identifier
  - enrollment_date: ISO format date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - progress: integer percentage (0-100)
  - status: enrollment status (e.g., In Progress, Completed)
- Example Lines:
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress

### 4. assignments.txt
- File Path: data/assignments.txt
- Format: assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points
- Fields:
  - assignment_id: unique assignment identifier (int)
  - course_id: related course identifier
  - title: assignment title
  - description: detailed description
  - due_date: ISO date for submission deadline
  - max_points: maximum points achievable (int)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200

### 5. submissions.txt
- File Path: data/submissions.txt
- Format: submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback
- Fields:
  - submission_id: unique submission identifier (int)
  - assignment_id: assignment identifier
  - username: submitting user
  - submission_text: text response submitted
  - submit_date: ISO date of submission
  - grade: numeric grade (int or empty)
  - feedback: text feedback (empty if none)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!

### 6. certificates.txt
- File Path: data/certificates.txt
- Format: certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date
- Fields:
  - certificate_id: unique certificate identifier (int)
  - username: user who earned certificate
  - course_id: course identifier
  - issue_date: ISO date certificate was issued
- Example Lines:
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort
from datetime import datetime
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['DATA_DIR'] = 'data'

# Helper functions for reading and writing files

def read_file(filename):
    path = os.path.join(app.config['DATA_DIR'], filename)
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return []
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        return [line.strip().split('|') for line in f if line.strip()]


def write_file(filename, lines):
    path = os.path.join(app.config['DATA_DIR'], filename)
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for line in lines:
            f.write('|'.join(str(x) for x in line) + '\n')


def get_user(username):
    users = read_file('users.txt')
    for u in users:
        if u[0] == username:
            return {'username': u[0], 'email': u[1], 'fullname': u[2]}
    return None


def get_courses():
    courses = read_file('courses.txt')
    res = []
    for c in courses:
        res.append({
            'course_id': int(c[0]),
            'title': c[1],
            'description': c[2],
            'category': c[3],
            'level': c[4],
            'duration': c[5],
            'status': c[6] if len(c) > 6 else ''
        })
    return res


def get_enrollments(username):
    enrolls = read_file('enrollments.txt')
    user_enrolls = []
    for e in enrolls:
        if e[1] == username:
            user_enrolls.append({
                'enrollment_id': int(e[0]),
                'username': e[1],
                'course_id': int(e[2]),
                'enroll_date': e[3],
                'progress': int(e[4]),
                'status': e[5]
            })
    return user_enrolls


def get_enrollment(username, course_id):
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    for e in enrollments:
        if e['course_id'] == course_id:
            return e
    return None


def save_enrollments(enrollments):
    lines = []
    for e in enrollments:
        lines.append([
            str(e['enrollment_id']), e['username'], str(e['course_id']), e['enroll_date'], str(e['progress']), e['status']
        ])
    write_file('enrollments.txt', lines)


def get_assignments():
    assigns = read_file('assignments.txt')
    res = []
    for a in assigns:
        res.append({
            'assignment_id': int(a[0]),
            'course_id': int(a[1]),
            'title': a[2],
            'description': a[3],
            'due_date': a[4],
            'max_points': int(a[5])
        })
    return res


def get_submissions():
    subs = read_file('submissions.txt')
    res = []
    for s in subs:
        res.append({
            'submission_id': s[0],
            'assignment_id': int(s[1]),
            'username': s[2],
            'submission_text': s[3],
            'submit_date': s[4],
            'grade': int(s[5]),
            'feedback': s[6] if len(s) > 6 else ''
        })
    return res


def save_submissions(submissions):
    lines = []
    for s in submissions:
        lines.append([
            s['submission_id'], str(s['assignment_id']), s['username'], s['submission_text'], s['submit_date'], str(s['grade']), s.get('feedback', '')
        ])
    write_file('submissions.txt', lines)


def get_certificates(username):
    certs = read_file('certificates.txt')
    res = []
    for c in certs:
        if c[1] == username:
            res.append({
                'certificate_id': int(c[0]),
                'username': c[1],
                'course_id': int(c[2]),
                'issue_date': c[3]
            })
    return res


def save_certificate(certificate):
    certs = read_file('certificates.txt')
    certs.append([
        str(certificate['certificate_id']),
        certificate['username'],
        str(certificate['course_id']),
        certificate['issue_date']
    ])
    write_file('certificates.txt', certs)


def get_next_enrollment_id():
    enrolls = read_file('enrollments.txt')
    if not enrolls:
        return 1
    return max(int(e[0]) for e in enrolls) + 1


def get_next_submission_id():
    subs = read_file('submissions.txt')
    if not subs:
        return '1'
    max_id = 0
    for s in subs:
        try:
            sid = int(s[0])
            if sid > max_id:
                max_id = sid
        except:
            continue
    return str(max_id + 1)


def get_next_certificate_id():
    certs = read_file('certificates.txt')
    if not certs:
        return 1
    return max(int(c[0]) for c in certs) + 1


@app.route('/')
def root():
    # Redirect to a default username dashboard for demonstration
    # Better approach: use session or login system
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard', username='john'))


@app.route('/dashboard/<username>')
def dashboard(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    courses = get_courses()
    enrolled_courses = []
    for e in enrollments:
        course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == e['course_id']), None)
        if course:
            enrolled_courses.append({
                'course_id': course['course_id'],
                'title': course['title'],
                'progress': e['progress']
            })
    return render_template('dashboard.html', fullname=user['fullname'], enrolled_courses=enrolled_courses)


@app.route('/catalog/<username>')
def catalog(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    courses = get_courses()
    simple_courses = [{'course_id': c['course_id'], 'title': c['title'], 'description': c['description']} for c in courses]
    return render_template('catalog.html', username=username, courses=simple_courses)


@app.route('/course/<username>/<int:course_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def course_details(username, course_id):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    courses = get_courses()
    course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == course_id), None)
    if not course:
        abort(404)

    enroll = get_enrollment(username, course_id)
    already_enrolled = enroll is not None

    if request.method == 'POST':
        if not already_enrolled:
            enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
            new_id = get_next_enrollment_id()
            now = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
            enrollments.append({
                'enrollment_id': new_id,
                'username': username,
                'course_id': course_id,
                'enroll_date': now,
                'progress': 0,
                'status': 'In Progress'
            })
            save_enrollments(enrollments)
            return redirect(url_for('my_courses', username=username))

    # If GET
    return render_template('course_details.html', username=username, course=course, already_enrolled=already_enrolled)


@app.route('/my-courses/<username>')
def my_courses(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    courses = get_courses()
    enrolled_courses = []
    for e in enrollments:
        course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == e['course_id']), None)
        if course:
            enrolled_courses.append({
                'course_id': course['course_id'],
                'title': course['title'],
                'progress': e['progress'],
                'status': e['status']
            })
    return render_template('my_courses.html', username=username, enrolled_courses=enrolled_courses)


@app.route('/learn/<username>/<int:course_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def course_learning(username, course_id):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    courses = get_courses()
    course = next((c for c in courses if c['course_id'] == course_id), None)
    if not course:
        abort(404)
    enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
    enrollment = next((e for e in enrollments if e['course_id'] == course_id), None)
    if not enrollment:
        abort(403) # Not enrolled

    # Dummy lessons list for demo
    lessons = [
        {'lesson_id': 1, 'title': 'Lesson 1', 'content': 'Content of lesson 1'},
        {'lesson_id': 2, 'title': 'Lesson 2', 'content': 'Content of lesson 2'},
        {'lesson_id': 3, 'title': 'Lesson 3', 'content': 'Content of lesson 3'},
    ]

    progress = enrollment['progress']
    # Determine current lesson index based on progress - 0,33,66 (integer division)
    current_index = progress // 33 if progress > 0 else 0
    if current_index >= len(lessons):
        current_index = len(lessons)-1
    current_lesson = lessons[current_index]

    # Determine if user can mark current lesson complete
    can_mark_complete = not (progress >= 100)

    if request.method == 'POST':
        if can_mark_complete and (progress < 100):
            progress = min(progress + 33, 100)
            enrollment['progress'] = progress
            if progress == 100:
                enrollment['status'] = 'Completed'
                # Issue certificate
                certs = get_certificates(username)
                already_cert = any(c['course_id'] == course_id for c in certs)
                if not already_cert:
                    cert_id = get_next_certificate_id()
                    issue_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                    certificate = {
                        'certificate_id': cert_id,
                        'username': username,
                        'course_id': course_id,
                        'issue_date': issue_date
                    }
                    save_certificate(certificate)
            enrollments = get_enrollments(username)
            # Update enrollment progress and status
            for i, e in enumerate(enrollments):
                if e['enrollment_id'] == enrollment['enrollment_id']:
                    enrollments[i]['progress'] = enrollment['progress']
                    enrollments[i]['status'] = enrollment.get('status', e['status'])
                    break
            save_enrollments(enrollments)

    complete = (progress == 100)

    return render_template('course_learning.html', username=username, course=course, lessons=lessons, current_lesson=current_lesson, progress=progress, complete=complete, can_mark_complete=can_mark_complete)


@app.route('/assignments/<username>')
def assignments(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    assigns = get_assignments()
    submissions = get_submissions()
    submissions_dict = {}
    for a in assigns:
        subm = None
        for s in submissions:
            if s['assignment_id'] == a['assignment_id'] and s['username'] == username:
                subm = s
                break
        submissions_dict[a['assignment_id']] = subm

    return render_template('assignments.html', username=username, assignments=assigns, submissions=submissions_dict)


@app.route('/submit-assignment/<username>/<int:assignment_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def submit_assignment(username, assignment_id):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    assigns = get_assignments()
    assignment = next((a for a in assigns if a['assignment_id'] == assignment_id), None)
    if not assignment:
        abort(404)

    if request.method == 'POST':
        submission_text = request.form.get('submission_text', '')
        submit_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
        subm_id = get_next_submission_id()
        submissions = get_submissions()
        # Add new submission or replace old one
        submissions = [s for s in submissions if not (s['assignment_id'] == assignment_id and s['username'] == username)]

        new_submission = {
            'submission_id': subm_id,
            'assignment_id': assignment_id,
            'username': username,
            'submission_text': submission_text,
            'submit_date': submit_date,
            'grade': 0,
            'feedback': ''
        }
        submissions.append(new_submission)
        save_submissions(submissions)
        return redirect(url_for('assignments', username=username))

    return render_template('submit_assignment.html', username=username, assignment=assignment)


@app.route('/certificates/<username>')
def certificates(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    certs = get_certificates(username)
    # Retrieve courses list to get titles for certificate display
    courses = get_courses()
    # Compose certificates as dict with title
    certificates_with_titles = []
    for c in certs:
        course = next((co for co in courses if co['course_id'] == c['course_id']), None)
        title = course['title'] if course else ''
        certificates_with_titles.append({
            'certificate_id': c['certificate_id'],
            'course_id': c['course_id'],
            'title': title,
            'issue_date': c['issue_date']
        })
    return render_template('certificates.html', username=username, certificates=certificates_with_titles)


@app.route('/profile/<username>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def profile(username):
    user = get_user(username)
    if not user:
        abort(404)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        fullname = request.form.get('fullname', '').strip()
        email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
        if fullname and email:
            users = read_file('users.txt')
            for i, u in enumerate(users):
                if u[0] == username:
                    users[i] = [username, email, fullname]
                    break
            write_file('users.txt', users)
            return redirect(url_for('profile', username=username))
        else:
            # possibly show an error or just reload
            pass
    return render_template('profile.html', username=username, fullname=user['fullname'], email=user['email'])


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

# Design Specification for OnlineCourse Web Application

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)

| Route Path                      | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template File            | Context Variables                                   |
|--------------------------------|-------------------------|-------------|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| /                              | root                    | GET         | N/A (redirect to dashboard) | None                                                |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard               | GET         | dashboard.html           | username: str, fullname: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int}) |
| /catalog                      | catalog                 | GET         | catalog.html             | username: str, courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str})                      |
| /course/<int:course_id>        | course_details          | GET, POST   | course_details.html      | username: str, course: dict ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str, category: str, level: str, duration: str, status: str}), already_enrolled: bool |
| /my-courses                   | my_courses              | GET         | my_courses.html          | username: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int, status: str})   |
| /learn/<int:course_id>          | course_learning         | GET, POST   | course_learning.html     | username: str, course: dict, lessons: list of dicts ({lesson_id: int, title: str, content: str}), current_lesson: dict, progress: int, can_mark_complete: bool |
| /assignments                  | my_assignments          | GET         | assignments.html         | username: str, assignments: list of dicts ({assignment_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, description: str, due_date: str, max_points: int}), submissions: dict {assignment_id: submission dict or None} |
| /submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id> | submit_assignment       | GET, POST   | submit_assignment.html   | username: str, assignment: dict ({assignment_id: int, title: str, description: str}), submission_status: str or None |
| /certificates                 | certificates            | GET         | certificates.html        | username: str, certificates: list of dicts ({certificate_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, issue_date: str}) |
| /profile                     | profile                 | GET, POST   | profile.html             | username: str, email: str, fullname: str |

### Route Behavior Notes:
- The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress.
- POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry.
- POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt.
- POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)

### 1. dashboard.html
- File Path: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Learning Dashboard (in <title> and <h1>)
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page (div container)
  - welcome-message (h1 displaying: "Welcome, {{ fullname }}")
  - enrolled-courses (div for listing enrolled courses)
  - browse-courses-button (button with url_for('catalog'))
  - my-courses-button (button with url_for('my_courses'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - fullname (str)
  - enrolled_courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, progress: int})
- Navigation:
  - browse-courses-button -> url_for('catalog')
  - my-courses-button -> url_for('my_courses')

### 2. catalog.html
- File Path: templates/catalog.html
- Page Title: Available Courses
- Element IDs:
  - catalog-page (div container)
  - search-input (input for search)
  - course-grid (div contains course cards)
  - view-course-button-{course_id} (button repeated for each course with id using Jinja: "view-course-button-{{ course.course_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, description: str})
- Navigation:
  - view-course-button-{course_id} -> url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

### 3. course_details.html

  - course-details-page (div container)
  - course-title (h1 showing course.title)

  - enroll-button (button)
  - back-to-catalog (button with url_for('catalog'))

  - enroll-button -> POST to url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)
  - enroll-button text: "Enroll" if not enrolled, "Already Enrolled" if enrolled
  - enroll-button disabled if already_enrolled == True
  - back-to-catalog -> url_for('catalog')

### 4. my_courses.html

  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

  - back-to-my-courses -> url_for('my_courses')

### 6. assignments.html

- Element IDs:

- Context Variables:

  - assignments (list of dicts: assignment_id, course_id, title, description, due_date, max_points)

- Page Title: Submit Assignment

- Form:
  - POST form to url_for('submit_assignment', assignment_id=assignment.assignment_id)

### 8. certificates.html
- File Path: templates/certificates.html
- Page Title: My Certificates

  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)

### 1. users.txt
- File Path: data/users.txt
- Format: username|email|fullname
- Fields:
  - username: user's unique login name
  - email: user email address
  - fullname: full name of user
- Example Lines:
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner

### 2. courses.txt
- File Path: data/courses.txt
- Format: course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status
- Fields:
  - course_id: unique course identifier (int)
  - title: course title
  - description: full course description
  - category: course category (e.g., Programming, Web, Data)
  - level: difficulty level (e.g., Beginner, Intermediate, Advanced)
  - duration: estimated course duration (e.g., "40 hours")
  - status: current course status (e.g., Active)
- Example Lines:
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active

### 3. enrollments.txt
- File Path: data/enrollments.txt
- Format: enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status
- Fields:
  - enrollment_id: unique enrollment identifier (int)
  - username: user login
  - course_id: course identifier
  - enrollment_date: ISO format date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - progress: integer percentage (0-100)
  - status: enrollment status (e.g., In Progress, Completed)
- Example Lines:
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress

### 4. assignments.txt
- File Path: data/assignments.txt
- Format: assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points
- Fields:
  - assignment_id: unique assignment identifier (int)
  - course_id: related course identifier
  - title: assignment title
  - description: detailed description
  - due_date: ISO date for submission deadline
  - max_points: maximum points achievable (int)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200

### 5. submissions.txt
- File Path: data/submissions.txt
- Format: submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback
- Fields:
  - submission_id: unique submission identifier (int)
  - assignment_id: assignment identifier
  - username: submitting user
  - submission_text: text response submitted
  - submit_date: ISO date of submission
  - grade: numeric grade (int or empty)
  - feedback: text feedback (empty if none)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!

### 6. certificates.txt
- File Path: data/certificates.txt
- Format: certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date
- Fields:
  - certificate_id: unique certificate identifier (int)
  - username: user who earned certificate
  - course_id: course identifier
  - issue_date: ISO date certificate was issued
- Example Lines:
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22

=== design_spec.md ===
# Design Specification for OnlineCourse Web Application

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)

| Route Path                      | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template File            | Context Variables                                   |
|--------------------------------|-------------------------|-------------|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| /                              | root                    | GET         | N/A (redirect to dashboard) | None                                                |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard               | GET         | dashboard.html           | username: str, fullname: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int}) |
| /catalog                      | catalog                 | GET         | catalog.html             | username: str, courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str})                      |
| /course/<int:course_id>        | course_details          | GET, POST   | course_details.html      | username: str, course: dict ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str, category: str, level: str, duration: str, status: str}), already_enrolled: bool |
| /my-courses                   | my_courses              | GET         | my_courses.html          | username: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int, status: str})   |
| /learn/<int:course_id>          | course_learning         | GET, POST   | course_learning.html     | username: str, course: dict, lessons: list of dicts ({lesson_id: int, title: str, content: str}), current_lesson: dict, progress: int, can_mark_complete: bool |
| /assignments                  | my_assignments          | GET         | assignments.html         | username: str, assignments: list of dicts ({assignment_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, description: str, due_date: str, max_points: int}), submissions: dict {assignment_id: submission dict or None} |
| /submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id> | submit_assignment       | GET, POST   | submit_assignment.html   | username: str, assignment: dict ({assignment_id: int, title: str, description: str}), submission_status: str or None |
| /certificates                 | certificates            | GET         | certificates.html        | username: str, certificates: list of dicts ({certificate_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, issue_date: str}) |
| /profile                     | profile                 | GET, POST   | profile.html             | username: str, email: str, fullname: str |

### Route Behavior Notes:
- The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress.
- POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry.
- POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt.
- POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)

### 1. dashboard.html
- File Path: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Learning Dashboard (in <title> and <h1>)
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page (div container)
  - welcome-message (h1 displaying: "Welcome, {{ fullname }}")
  - enrolled-courses (div for listing enrolled courses)
  - browse-courses-button (button with url_for('catalog'))
  - my-courses-button (button with url_for('my_courses'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - fullname (str)
  - enrolled_courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, progress: int})
- Navigation:
  - browse-courses-button -> url_for('catalog')
  - my-courses-button -> url_for('my_courses')

### 2. catalog.html
- File Path: templates/catalog.html
- Page Title: Available Courses
- Element IDs:
  - catalog-page (div container)
  - search-input (input for search)
  - course-grid (div contains course cards)
  - view-course-button-{course_id} (button repeated for each course with id using Jinja: "view-course-button-{{ course.course_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - courses (list of dicts: {course_id: int, title: str, description: str})
- Navigation:
  - view-course-button-{course_id} -> url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

### 3. course_details.html
- File Path: templates/course_details.html
- Page Title: Course Details
- Element IDs:
  - course-details-page (div container)
  - course-title (h1 showing course.title)
  - course-description (div showing course.description)
  - enroll-button (button)
  - back-to-catalog (button with url_for('catalog'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - course (dict with course data fields)
  - already_enrolled (bool)
- Navigation & Button State:
  - enroll-button -> POST to url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)
  - enroll-button text: "Enroll" if not enrolled, "Already Enrolled" if enrolled
  - enroll-button disabled if already_enrolled == True
  - back-to-catalog -> url_for('catalog')

### 4. my_courses.html
- File Path: templates/my_courses.html
- Page Title: My Courses
- Element IDs:
  - my-courses-page (div container)
  - courses-list (div listing enrolled courses)
  - continue-learning-button-{course_id} (button repeated; id="continue-learning-button-{{ course.course_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - enrolled_courses (list of dicts with course_id, title, progress, status)
- Navigation:
  - continue-learning-button-{course_id} -> url_for('course_learning', course_id=course.course_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')

### 5. course_learning.html
- File Path: templates/course_learning.html
- Page Title: Course Learning
- Element IDs:
  - learning-page (div container)
  - lessons-list (div listing lessons)
  - lesson-content (div showing current lesson content)
  - mark-complete-button (button)
  - back-to-my-courses (button with url_for('my_courses'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - course (dict)
  - lessons (list of dicts with lesson_id:int, title:str, content:str)
  - current_lesson (dict with lesson_id, title, content)
  - progress (int)
  - can_mark_complete (bool)
- Navigation & Button State:
  - mark-complete-button -> POST to url_for('course_learning', course_id=course.course_id)
  - mark-complete-button disabled if can_mark_complete == False
  - back-to-my-courses -> url_for('my_courses')

### 6. assignments.html
- File Path: templates/assignments.html
- Page Title: My Assignments
- Element IDs:
  - assignments-page (div container)
  - assignments-table (table containing assignments)
  - submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id} (button repeated; id="submit-assignment-button-{{ assignment.assignment_id }}")
  - back-to-dashboard (button with url_for('dashboard'))
- Context Variables:
  - username (str)
  - assignments (list of dicts: assignment_id, course_id, title, description, due_date, max_points)
  - submissions (dict with assignment_id keys, values: submission dict or None)
- Navigation:
  - submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id} -> url_for('submit_assignment', assignment_id=assignment.assignment_id)
  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')
- Button State:
  - submit-assignment-button is enabled only if assignment submission is not done yet or is late

### 7. submit_assignment.html

### 1. users.txt

- Format: username|email|fullname
- Fields:
  - username: user's unique login name
  - email: user email address
  - fullname: full name of user

  john|john@student.com|John Student

- File Path: data/courses.txt
- Format: course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status
- Fields:
  - course_id: unique course identifier (int)
  - title: course title
  - description: full course description
  - category: course category (e.g., Programming, Web, Data)
  - level: difficulty level (e.g., Beginner, Intermediate, Advanced)
  - duration: estimated course duration (e.g., "40 hours")
  - status: current course status (e.g., Active)
- Example Lines:
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active

- File Path: data/enrollments.txt
- Format: enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status
- Fields:
  - enrollment_id: unique enrollment identifier (int)
  - username: user login
  - course_id: course identifier
  - enrollment_date: ISO format date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - progress: integer percentage (0-100)
  - status: enrollment status (e.g., In Progress, Completed)
- Example Lines:
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress

### 4. assignments.txt
- File Path: data/assignments.txt
- Format: assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points
- Fields:
  - assignment_id: unique assignment identifier (int)
  - course_id: related course identifier
  - title: assignment title
  - description: detailed description
  - due_date: ISO date for submission deadline
  - max_points: maximum points achievable (int)
- Example Lines:
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200

### 5. submissions.txt
- File Path: data/submissions.txt
- Format: submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback
- Fields:
  - submission_id: unique submission identifier (int)
  - assignment_id: assignment identifier
  - username: submitting user
  - submission_text: text response submitted
  - submit_date: ISO date of submission
  - grade: numeric grade (int or empty)

- Example Lines:

  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!

=== design_spec.md ===
# Design Specification for OnlineCourse Web Application

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)

| Route Path                      | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template File            | Context Variables                                   |
|--------------------------------|-------------------------|-------------|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| /                              | root                    | GET         | N/A (redirect to dashboard) | None                                                |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard               | GET         | dashboard.html           | username: str, fullname: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int}) |
| /catalog                      | catalog                 | GET         | catalog.html             | username: str, courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str})                      |
| /course/<int:course_id>        | course_details          | GET, POST   | course_details.html      | username: str, course: dict ({course_id: int, title: str, description: str, category: str, level: str, duration: str, status: str}), already_enrolled: bool |
| /my-courses                   | my_courses              | GET         | my_courses.html          | username: str, enrolled_courses: list of dicts ({course_id: int, title: str, progress: int, status: str})   |
| /learn/<int:course_id>          | course_learning         | GET, POST   | course_learning.html     | username: str, course: dict, lessons: list of dicts ({lesson_id: int, title: str, content: str}), current_lesson: dict, progress: int, can_mark_complete: bool |
| /assignments                  | my_assignments          | GET         | assignments.html         | username: str, assignments: list of dicts ({assignment_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, description: str, due_date: str, max_points: int}), submissions: dict {assignment_id: submission dict or None} |
| /submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id> | submit_assignment       | GET, POST   | submit_assignment.html   | username: str, assignment: dict ({assignment_id: int, title: str, description: str}), submission_status: str or None |
| /certificates                 | certificates            | GET         | certificates.html        | username: str, certificates: list of dicts ({certificate_id: int, course_id: int, title: str, issue_date: str}) |
| /profile                     | profile                 | GET, POST   | profile.html             | username: str, email: str, fullname: str |

### Route Behavior Notes:
- The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
- POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress.
- POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry.
- POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt.
- POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)

### 1. dashboard.html
- File Path: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Learning Dashboard (in <title> and <h1>)
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page (div container)

Route Behavior Notes: - The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`. - POST `/course/<course_id>` enrolls the user if not already enrolled, updates enrollments.txt with enrollment date and 0% progress. - POST `/learn/<course_id>` marks current lesson complete if allowed, updates progress and enrollments.txt; if progress reaches 100%, creates certificate entry. - POST `/submit-assignment/<assignment_id>` records submission with "Submitted" status and current date in submissions.txt. - POST `/profile` updates user's email and fullname in users.txt.  ---  ## Section
